<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Variations on an Original Theme
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Enigma Variations
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Elgar,_Edward" title="Category:Elgar, Edward">Elgar, Edward</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.36
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IEE 91
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>15 sections
<dl><dd>Theme (Andante)
</dd><dd>Variation I. L'istesso tempo "C.A.E."
</dd><dd>Variation II. Allegro "H.D.S-P."
</dd><dd>Variation III. Allegretto "R.B.T."
</dd><dd>Variation IV. Allegro di molto "W.M.B."
</dd><dd>Variation V. Moderato "R.P.A."
</dd><dd>Variation VI. Andantino "Ysobel"
</dd><dd>Variation VII. Presto "Troyte"
</dd><dd>Variation VIII. Allegretto "W.N."
</dd><dd>Variation IX. Adagio "Nimrod"
</dd><dd>Variation X. Intermezzo: Allegretto "Dorabella"
</dd><dd>Variation XI. Allegro di molto "G.R.S."
</dd><dd>Variation XII. Andante "B.G.N."
</dd><dd>Variation XIII. Romanza: Moderato "* * *"
</dd><dd>Variation XIV. Finale: Allegro Presto "E.D.U."
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1899
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1899-06-18 in London, St. James Hall.
<dl><dd>Orchestra, Hans Richter (conductor)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1899
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>"To my friends pictured within"
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>32 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Early_20th_century" title="Category:Early 20th century">Early 20th century</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes (2nd also piccolo), 2 oboes, 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 2 bassoons,<br />contrabassoon, 4 horns (F), 3 trumpets (F), 3 trombones, tuba<br />timpani, triangle, small drum, cymbals, bass drum, organ ad lib., strings
</td></tr>
